#General
	#GetDollar
		defined_text = {
			name = GetDollar
			text = {
				localization_key = "$$"
			}
		}
	#GetRed
		defined_text = {
			name = GetRed
			text = {

#Infrastructure
#Graphs
	#State List
		#GetGraphStartYear
			defined_text = {
				name = GetGraphStartYear
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { year_temp = global.current_year }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { year_temp = 2 }
						check_variable = { year_temp > 0 }
					}
					localization_key = "[?year_temp|0]"
				}
			}
		#GetGraphMiddleYear
			defined_text = {
				name = GetGraphMiddleYear
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { year_temp = global.current_year }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { year_temp = 1 }
						check_variable = { year_temp > 0 }
					}
					localization_key = "[?year_temp|0]"
				}
			}


#Overview
	#GetGDPAmount
		defined_text = {
			name = GetGDPAmount
			text = {
				trigger = {
					check_variable = { selected_state:num_owned_states > 0 } #A way of checking if it's a country scope or not
				}
				localization_key = "[GetNationalGDPAmount]"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					check_variable = { selected_state:gdp_this_year > 1000 }
					set_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = selected_state:gdp_this_year }
					divide_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = 1000 }
				}
				localization_key = "$[?gdp_amount_temp|3]K"
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "$[?selected_state:gdp_this_year|3]"
			}
		}
		defined_text = {
			name = GetNationalGDPAmount
			text = {
				trigger = {
					check_variable = { selected_state:gdp_this_year < 1 }
					set_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = selected_state:gdp_this_year }
					multiply_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = 1000 }
				}
				localization_key = "$[?gdp_amount_temp|0]"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					check_variable = { selected_state:gdp_this_year > 1000 }
					set_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = selected_state:gdp_this_year }
					divide_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = 1000 }
				}
				localization_key = "$[?gdp_amount_temp|3]M"
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "$[?selected_state:gdp_this_year|3]K"
			}
		}
	#
	#GetGDPChange
		defined_text = {
			name = GetGDPChange
			#text = {
			#	trigger = {
			#		check_variable = { selected_state:num_owned_states > 0 } #A way of checking if it's a country scope or not
			#	}
			#	localization_key = "[GetNationalGDPChange]"
			#}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					check_variable = { selected_state:gdp_change < -1000 }
					set_temp_variable = { gdp_temp = selected_state:gdp_change }
					divide_temp_variable = { gdp_temp = -1000 }
				}
				localization_key = "-$[?gdp_temp|0]K"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					check_variable = { selected_state:gdp_change < -1 }
					set_temp_variable = { gdp_temp = selected_state:gdp_change }
					divide_temp_variable = { gdp_temp = -1 }
				}
				localization_key = "-$[?gdp_temp|3]"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					check_variable = { selected_state:gdp_change = 0 }
				}
				localization_key = "+0"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					check_variable = { selected_state:gdp_change > 1000 }
					set_temp_variable = { gdp_temp = selected_state:gdp_change }
					divide_temp_variable = { gdp_temp = 1000 }
				}
				localization_key = "+$[?gdp_temp|3]K"
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "+$[?selected_state:gdp_change|3]"
			}
		}
		defined_text = {
			name = GetGDPChangeColor
			text = {
				trigger = {
					check_variable = { selected_state:gdp_change < 0 }
				}
				localization_key = "red"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					check_variable = { selected_state:gdp_change > 0 }
				}
				localization_key = "green"
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "yellow"
			}
		}

					}
					localization_key = "[?giucc|+=0]"
				}
			}
			defined_text = {
				name = GetIndustriesUnderConstruction0TextIcon
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { giuc = selected_state:industries_under_construction_array^0 }
						set_temp_variable = { giucc = global.industry_resource_output@var:giuc }
					}

				}
			}

								limit = {
									check_variable = { global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_6@var:v > 0 }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_6@var:v }

								set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_6@var:v }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = selected_state:price@var:gip_imr }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = maintenance_modifier_temp }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
								subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_7@var:v > 0 }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_7@var:v }

								set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_7@var:v }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = selected_state:price@var:gip_imr }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = maintenance_modifier_temp }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
								subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_8@var:v > 0 }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_8@var:v }

								set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_8@var:v }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = selected_state:price@var:gip_imr }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = maintenance_modifier_temp }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
								subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
							}

							set_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.industry_base_laborers_employment@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.industry_base_workers_employment@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.industry_base_professionals_employment@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.industry_base_elites_employment@var:v }
							divide_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_employees }

							check_variable = { gip_profit > 0 }
						}
						localization_key = "[GetGreen]$[?gip_profit|3]"
					}
					text = {
						trigger = {
							check_variable = { gip_profit < 0 }
						}
						localization_key = "[GetRed]$[?gip_profit|3]"
					}
					text = {
						localization_key = "[GetYellow]$[?gip_profit|3]"
					}
				}

							add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }
							set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = selected_state:throughput_factor@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_v = global.industry_base_output@var:v }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_v = selected_state:size@var:v }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_v = output_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_v = throughput_modifier_temp }
						}
						localization_key = "[?gip_v|3]"

					text = {
						trigger = {
							set_temp_variable = { gip_res = global.industry_resource_output@var:v }

							set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = selected_state:output_factor@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

							set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = selected_state:throughput_factor@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

							set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = selected_state:input_factor@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

							set_temp_variable = { maintenance_modifier_temp = selected_state:maintenance_factor@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { maintenance_modifier_temp = 1 }

							#Revenue
							set_temp_variable = { gip_profit = selected_state:price@var:gip_res }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = global.industry_industrialized_output@var:v }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = output_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = throughput_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = selected_state:size@var:v }

							#Expenses
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { global.industry_industrialized_input_amount_1@var:v > 0 }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.industry_industrialized_input_resource_1@var:v }

								set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.industry_industrialized_input_amount_1@var:v }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = selected_state:price@var:gip_imr }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = selected_state:size@var:v }
								subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { global.industry_industrialized_input_amount_2@var:v > 0 }

								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = selected_state:price@var:gip_imr }

								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }

							add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

							set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = selected_state:input_factor@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

							set_temp_variable = { maintenance_modifier_temp = selected_state:maintenance_factor@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { maintenance_modifier_temp = 1 }

							#Revenue
							set_temp_variable = { gip_profit = selected_state:price@var:gip_res }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = global.industry_mechanized_output@var:v }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = output_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = throughput_modifier_temp }

								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = selected_state:price@var:gip_imr }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
								subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

							add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

							set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = selected_state:throughput_factor@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = output_modifier_temp }

								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = maintenance_modifier_temp }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
								subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { global.industry_modernized_maintenance_amount_4@var:v > 0 }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.industry_modernized_maintenance_resource_4@var:v }

								set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.industry_modernized_maintenance_amount_4@var:v }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = selected_state:price@var:gip_imr }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = maintenance_modifier_temp }
								multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
								subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

							add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.industry_modernized_workers_employment@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.industry_modernized_professionals_employment@var:v }
							add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.industry_modernized_elites_employment@var:v }
							divide_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_employees }

							check_variable = { gip_profit > 0 }
						}
						localization_key = "[GetGreen]$[?gip_profit|3]"
					}
					text = {
						trigger = {
							check_variable = { gip_profit < 0 }

		#GetIndustryEmploymentIcon
			defined_text = {
				name = GetIndustryEmploymentIcon
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { emp_frame = selected_state:employment_percentage@var:v }
						check_variable = { emp_frame = 0 }
					}
					localization_key = "GFX_employment_icon_none"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { emp_frame = selected_state:employment_percentage@var:v }
						multiply_temp_variable = { emp_frame = 100 }
						divide_temp_variable = { emp_frame = 10 }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { emp_frame < 1 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { emp_frame = 1 }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { emp_frame < 10 }
								check_variable = { emp_frame > 9 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { emp_frame = 9 }
						}
						round_temp_variable = emp_frame
					}
					localization_key = "GFX_employment_icon_[?emp_frame]"
				}
			}

#Market Capital
	#GetMarketCapitalText
		defined_text = {

				trigger = {
					check_variable = { selected_market = selected_state }

			}
			text = {
				trigger = {

						check_variable = { selected_state > 0 }

							check_variable = { controller:market_capital = THIS }
						}
					}
				}
				localization_key = market_capital_button_text_view
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = market_capital_button_text_goto
			}
